251214 git
=================

# TIL
- git can be set up for SSH keys.
- it use git remote by 'git@github.com:~'
- git remote set-url origin [github https]
- and I can set up token251214 git

- it use git remote by 'git@github.com:~'
- git remote set-url origin [github https]
- and I can set up token251214 git

- it use git remote by 'git@github.com:~'
- git remote set-url origin [github https]
- and I can set up token251214 git

- it use git remote by 'git@github.com:~'
- git remote set-url origin [github https]
- and I can set up token251214 git

- it use git remote by 'git@github.com:~'
- git remote set-url origin [github https]
- and I can set up token251214 git

- it use git remote by 'git@github.com:~'
- git remote set-url origin [github https]
- and I can set up token251214 git

- it use git remote by 'git@github.com:~'
- git remote set-url origin [github https]
- and I can set up token251214 git

- and I can set up token251214 git
=================
